<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">Economy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Economy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Update plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Update" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><img alt="Ambox current red.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/42px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png" decoding="async" width="42" height="34" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/63px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/84px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="360" data-file-height="290" /></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section's <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Accuracy_dispute" title="Wikipedia:Accuracy dispute">factual accuracy</a> may be compromised due to out-of-date information</b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">March 2019</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Refiner%C3%ADa_de_Amuay_VE.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Refiner%C3%ADa_de_Amuay_VE.jpg/220px-Refiner%C3%ADa_de_Amuay_VE.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Refiner%C3%ADa_de_Amuay_VE.jpg/330px-Refiner%C3%ADa_de_Amuay_VE.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Refiner%C3%ADa_de_Amuay_VE.jpg/440px-Refiner%C3%ADa_de_Amuay_VE.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3200" data-file-height="1800" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Refiner%C3%ADa_de_Amuay_VE.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Paraguan%C3%A1_Refinery_Complex" title="Paraguaná Refinery Complex">Paraguaná Refinery Complex</a>, considered the second largest and largest capacity in the world.</div></div></div>
<p>The economy of UNASUR is divided between the mineral extractivism in the Amazon region and the agriculture present in practically all its States. Industrialization is of medium level to high in diverse regions, although very strong the presence of local industries of origin Foreign (multinational). The extraction and export of oil is notable in Venezuela, which owns the largest world reserves. Bolivia stands out for the production of natural gas, with important reserves of this matter that in recent years have led to what has been known as the "Gas War."
</p><p>The highest <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(nominal)" title="List of countries by GDP (nominal)">nominal GDP</a> in 2018 is Venezuela (62nd worldwide) with 96,328&#160;billion dollars, followed by Uruguay (73rd worldwide) with 60,933&#160;billion dollars, and Bolivia (92nd at the global level) with 41,833&#160;billion dollars.
</p><p>The highest <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(PPP)" title="List of countries by GDP (PPP)">GDP</a> in 2018 is in Venezuela (52nd worldwide) with 330,984&#160;billion dollars, Bolivia (88th worldwide) with 88,866&#160;billion dollars, and Uruguay (91st Worldwide) with 82,641&#160;billion dollars.
</p><p>The highest <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(PPP)_per_capita" title="List of countries by GDP (PPP) per capita">GDP per capita</a> in 2018 is held by Uruguay with US$22,445, followed by Suriname with 13,876 and Venezuela with 12,388. In terms of <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_GDP_(nominal)_per_capita" title="List of countries by GDP (nominal) per capita">nominal per capita GDP</a>, the ranking is headed by Uruguay with US$16,641, Venezuela with US$6,890, and Suriname with US$5,869.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Common_Market">Common Market</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Common Market">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Initiative_for_the_Integration_of_the_Regional_Infrastructure_of_South_America" title="Initiative for the Integration of the Regional Infrastructure of South America">Initiative for the Integration of the Regional Infrastructure of South America</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Map_of_member_states_of_unasur_english.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Map_of_member_states_of_unasur_english.svg/180px-Map_of_member_states_of_unasur_english.svg.png" decoding="async" width="180" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Map_of_member_states_of_unasur_english.svg/270px-Map_of_member_states_of_unasur_english.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/67/Map_of_member_states_of_unasur_english.svg/360px-Map_of_member_states_of_unasur_english.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="744" data-file-height="1052" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Map_of_member_states_of_unasur_english.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Members of UNASUR and main regional highways.</div></div></div>
<p>One of the initiatives of Unasur is the creation of a <a href="/wiki/Common_market" class="mw-redirect" title="Common market">common market</a>, starting with the elimination of <a href="/wiki/Tariffs" class="mw-redirect" title="Tariffs">tariffs</a> for products considered non-sensitive until 2014 and for sensitive products until 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Initiative_for_the_Integration_of_the_Regional_Infrastructure_of_South_America" title="Initiative for the Integration of the Regional Infrastructure of South America">Initiative for the Integration of the Regional Infrastructure of South America</a> is currently underway, with investments estimated at US$38&#160;billion from the <a href="/wiki/Inter-American_Development_Bank" title="Inter-American Development Bank">Inter-American Development Bank</a>, the Andean Development Corporation, the <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Development_Bank" title="Brazilian Development Bank">National Bank for Economic and Social Development</a> and the Financial Fund for Development of the Plata Basin.<sup id="cite_ref-Integração_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Integração-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The initial integration plans through the infrastructure cooperation of UNASUR came with the construction of the Bioceanic Corridor and the <a href="/wiki/Interoceanic_Highway" title="Interoceanic Highway">Interoceanic Highway</a>. The Pacific Highway, between Peru and Brazil, began to be built in September 2005, financed 60% by Brazil and 40% by Peru, and was completed in December 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-Integração_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Integração-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Economic_development">Economic development</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Economic development">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:GDP_PPP_2018_Selection.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/GDP_PPP_2018_Selection.svg/250px-GDP_PPP_2018_Selection.svg.png" decoding="async" width="250" height="250" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/GDP_PPP_2018_Selection.svg/375px-GDP_PPP_2018_Selection.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/GDP_PPP_2018_Selection.svg/500px-GDP_PPP_2018_Selection.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="512" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:GDP_PPP_2018_Selection.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Selection of GDP PPP data (top 10 countries and blocks) in no particular order</div></div></div>
<p>Presidents of the seven founding countries (Argentina, Bolivia, Brazil, Ecuador, Paraguay, Venezuela and Uruguay) officially launched the South American Bank in Buenos Aires in December 2007.  The heads of all the founding countries were at the ceremony, with the exception of President <a href="/wiki/Tabar%C3%A9_V%C3%A1zquez" title="Tabaré Vázquez">Tabaré Vázquez</a> of Uruguay. The capital will be US$7b, with Venezuela responsible for US$3b and Brazil US$2b. The headquarters will be located in Caracas with offices in Buenos Aires and La Paz.<sup id="cite_ref-MercoPress1_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MercoPress1-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-bbc1_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bbc1-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_the_South" title="Bank of the South">Bank of the South</a> will finance economic development projects to improve local competitiveness and to promote the scientific and technological development of the member states. Its founding charter affirms that the bank will promote projects in a "stable and equal" manner and priorities will be oriented towards reinforcing South American integration, reducing asymmetries, and promoting an egalitarian distribution of investments.
</p><p>The Brazilian Minister, Guido Mantega, stated that the bank is not similar to the <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a>; it will be a credit institution similar to the <a href="/wiki/World_Bank" title="World Bank">World Bank</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Monetary_policy">Monetary policy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Monetary policy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Single_South_American_currency" title="Single South American currency">Single South American currency</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_the_South" title="Bank of the South">Bank of the South</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Banco_del_Sur.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Banco_del_Sur.jpg/250px-Banco_del_Sur.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="172" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Banco_del_Sur.jpg/375px-Banco_del_Sur.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3b/Banco_del_Sur.jpg/500px-Banco_del_Sur.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2100" data-file-height="1442" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Banco_del_Sur.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Rafael_Correa" title="Rafael Correa">Rafael Correa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Evo_Morales" title="Evo Morales">Evo Morales</a>, <a href="/wiki/N%C3%A9stor_Kirchner" title="Néstor Kirchner">Néstor Kirchner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cristina_Fern%C3%A1ndez" class="mw-redirect" title="Cristina Fernández">Cristina Fernández</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luiz_In%C3%A1cio_Lula_da_Silva" title="Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva">Luiz Inácio Lula da Silva</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nicanor_Duarte" title="Nicanor Duarte">Nicanor Duarte</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> at the signing of the founding charter of the Bank of the South</div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_the_South" title="Bank of the South">Bank of the South</a> (Portuguese: Banco do Sul, Spanish: Banco del Sur, Dutch: Bank van het Zuiden, English: Bank of the South) will establish monetary policy and finance development projects. One of the objectives of monetary union is to establish a <a href="/wiki/Single_South_American_currency" title="Single South American currency">Single South American currency</a>. Support for the creation of this currency was provided in January 2007 by Peruvian President <a href="/wiki/Alan_Garc%C3%ADa" title="Alan García">Alan García</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> and other South American authorities expressed themselves in favor, as Bolivian President <a href="/wiki/Evo_Morales" title="Evo Morales">Evo Morales</a> in April of that year, who proposed that the currency Only one denominated "Pacha" ("earth" in <a href="/wiki/Quechua_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Quechua language">Quechua language</a>), however, except for the right of each country to suggest a name for the common currency.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Defense_policy">Defense policy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Defense policy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Update plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Update" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><img alt="Ambox current red.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/42px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png" decoding="async" width="42" height="34" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/63px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/84px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="360" data-file-height="290" /></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section's <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Accuracy_dispute" title="Wikipedia:Accuracy dispute">factual accuracy</a> may be compromised due to out-of-date information</b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">March 2019</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/South_American_Defense_Council" class="mw-redirect" title="South American Defense Council">South American Defense Council</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Unasul_1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Unasul_1.jpg/220px-Unasul_1.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="142" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Unasul_1.jpg/330px-Unasul_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Unasul_1.jpg/440px-Unasul_1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1835" data-file-height="1185" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Unasul_1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Soldier of the <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Army" title="Brazilian Army">Brazilian Army</a> patrols the surroundings of the Summit of Heads of State of Unasur in 2008, held in Brasilia.</div></div></div>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/South_American_Defense_Council" class="mw-redirect" title="South American Defense Council">South American Defense Council</a> (CDS) was proposed by Venezuela and Brazil to serve as a mechanism for regional security, promoting military co-operation. From the beginning Brazil, Argentina and Chile, the countries that took the leadership of the project, made clear that they did not intend to form a <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a>-like alliance, but a cooperative security arrangement, enhancing multilateral military cooperation, promoting confidence and security building measures and fostering defense industry exchange. Colombia initially refused to join the defense council due to the strong military ties it has with the United States through the <a href="/wiki/Plan_Colombia" title="Plan Colombia">Plan Colombia</a>. However, after reviewing the proposal they decided to join on 20 July 2008.<sup id="cite_ref-ecodiario1_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ecodiario1-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-people1_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-people1-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Shortly following the signing by Colombia's President, President of Chile <a href="/wiki/Michelle_Bachelet" title="Michelle Bachelet">Michelle Bachelet</a> appointed a working group to investigate and draft a plan for the new council. Finally, on 10 March 2009, the 12 nation members held, in Chile, the first meeting of the newly formed council.<sup id="cite_ref-coha1_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-coha1-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In mid-2010, UNASUR played a key role in mediating the <a href="/wiki/2010_Colombia%E2%80%93Venezuela_diplomatic_crisis" title="2010 Colombia–Venezuela diplomatic crisis">2010 Colombia–Venezuela diplomatic crisis</a>. On 1 September 2010, the agency "UnasurHaití" was created to provide US$100&#160;million in help to Haiti.<sup id="cite_ref-pagina12_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pagina12-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Democracy">Democracy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Democracy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Update plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Update" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><img alt="Ambox current red.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/42px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png" decoding="async" width="42" height="34" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/63px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/84px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="360" data-file-height="290" /></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section's <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Accuracy_dispute" title="Wikipedia:Accuracy dispute">factual accuracy</a> may be compromised due to out-of-date information</b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">March 2019</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bicentenario_Argentina_-_Presidentes.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Bicentenario_Argentina_-_Presidentes.jpg/220px-Bicentenario_Argentina_-_Presidentes.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Bicentenario_Argentina_-_Presidentes.jpg/330px-Bicentenario_Argentina_-_Presidentes.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7e/Bicentenario_Argentina_-_Presidentes.jpg/440px-Bicentenario_Argentina_-_Presidentes.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3312" data-file-height="2490" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bicentenario_Argentina_-_Presidentes.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>South American presidents in front of the <a href="/wiki/Casa_Rosada" title="Casa Rosada">Casa Rosada</a>, Buenos Aires, during the bicentenary of the <a href="/wiki/May_Revolution" title="May Revolution">May Revolution</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>On 26 November 2010, the Additional Protocol on Commitment to Democracy was signed in the city of <a href="/wiki/Georgetown,_Guyana" title="Georgetown, Guyana">Georgetown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cooperative_Republic_of_Guyana" class="mw-redirect" title="Cooperative Republic of Guyana">Cooperative Republic of Guyana</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> The protocol derives from the mandate established in the Buenos Aires Declaration of 1 October 2010, which affirms that member states will not tolerate a challenge to institutional authority, nor attempt to strike a legitimately constituted civilian power, adopting concrete and immediate measures in case of breach of constitutional order. It is applicable "in the event of a breach or threat of a breach of the democratic order, of a violation of the constitutional order or in any situation that endangers the legitimate exercise of power and the observance of democratic values and principles."<sup id="cite_ref-Democracia_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Democracia-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the event of such a situation, the Council of Heads of State and Government or the Council of Ministers of Foreign Affairs may be convened extraordinarily by the Pro-Tempore Presidency of the Union, ex officio or at the request of the affected State or another member of UNASUR, to deliberate on the application of sanctions to the affected state. Among the political and diplomatic sanctions envisaged by the Protocol, the following stand out:<sup id="cite_ref-Democracia_77-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Democracia-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<ul><li>Suspension of the right to participate in the different organs and instances of Unasur<sup id="cite_ref-Democracia_77-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Democracia-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Partial or total closure of land borders with the affected State, including suspension or limitation of trade, air and sea transportation, communications, energy supply, services and supply.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Free_movement_of_people">Free movement of people</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Free movement of people">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<table class="box-Update plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Update" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><img alt="Ambox current red.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/42px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png" decoding="async" width="42" height="34" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/63px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/84px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="360" data-file-height="290" /></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section's <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Accuracy_dispute" title="Wikipedia:Accuracy dispute">factual accuracy</a> may be compromised due to out-of-date information</b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.</span>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">March 2019</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>Visits by citizens of UNASUR to any other UNASUR member state of up to 90 days only require an identification document issued by the traveler's country. In November 2006, Argentina, Bolivia, Brazil, Chile, Colombia, Ecuador, Guyana, Paraguay, Peru, Suriname, and Uruguay agreed to abolish visa requirements for tourists between any of those nations.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Mercosur, along with its Associate members of Bolivia, Chile, Colombia and Ecuador established that their territories together form an "area of free residence with the right to work" to all its citizens, with no additional requirements other than nationality. The Free Movement and Residence Agreement was established in the <a href="/wiki/Bras%C3%ADlia" title="Brasília">Brasília</a> summit based in a previous document signed on 6 December 2002.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Citizens of any Mercosur countries will have a simplified process in temporary residence visa of up to two years in any other member countries, with the requirements of a valid passport, <a href="/wiki/Birth_certificate" title="Birth certificate">birth certificate</a>, and no criminal record. Temporary residence can become permanent if a licit means of living can be verified.
</p><p>At a summit in Guayaquil, Ecuador on 4 December 2014, UNASUR general secretary Ernesto Samper announced, "We have approved the concept of South American citizenship," including the creation of a single passport.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Electoral_monitors">Electoral monitors</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Electoral monitors">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>UNASUR intended to create <a href="/wiki/Election_monitoring" title="Election monitoring">electoral monitor teams</a> that would replace the monitors from the <a href="/wiki/Organization_of_American_States" title="Organization of American States">Organization of American States</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Participating_nation_states">Participating nation states</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Participating nation states">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

Considering them, the total area reaches the 29 884 548 km².</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participating_non-South_American_territories">Participating non-South American territories</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Participating non-South American territories">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The following territories situated outside South America are part of member states and therefore participate:
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Isla_Aves" class="mw-redirect" title="Isla Aves">Isla Aves</a>, a Venezuelan territory situated in the <a href="/wiki/Antilles" title="Antilles">Antilles</a>.</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Non-participating_South_American_states_and_territories">Non-participating South American states and territories</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Non-participating South American states and territories">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The following parts of South America are or were territories of non-South American states and therefore do not participate:
</p>
<ul><li>Aruba, <a href="/wiki/Bonaire" title="Bonaire">Bonaire</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao" title="Curaçao">Curaçao</a> are parts of the Kingdom of the Netherlands near the Venezuelan coastline.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/French_Guiana" title="French Guiana">French Guiana</a>, which is an <a href="/wiki/Overseas_department" class="mw-redirect" title="Overseas department">overseas department</a> of France and is therefore part of the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Georgia_and_the_South_Sandwich_Islands" title="South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands">South Georgia and the South Sandwich Islands</a>, which are <a href="/wiki/British_overseas_territory" class="mw-redirect" title="British overseas territory">overseas territories</a> of the United Kingdom<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Special_Member_State_territories_and_the_European_Union#Overseas_countries_and_territories" class="mw-redirect" title="Special Member State territories and the European Union">overseas countries and territories</a> of the European Union;<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> they are also claimed by Argentina.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Trinidad and Tobago, although not a member, this sovereign state had been a dependency of Great Britain and was invited to join the Union of South American Nations by President of Venezuela, <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Maduro" class="mw-redirect" title="Nicolas Maduro">Nicolas Maduro</a> in July 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
